Male Respondent File Codebook :: SECTION D: Recent (Or Last) Sexual Partner(s) and First Sexual Partner :: (DB) Key dates for former wives or partners who were also recent or last partners

MARDATEN_Y(710-713)

Variable Type : raw

DB-1y : (In what month and year were you and she married?) (Year) (MOST RECENT PARTNER)

value label   Total
. INAPPLICABLE   5116
1967-2019 1967-2019   87
9998 Refused   2
9999 Don't know   1
  Total   5206

Universe : Applicable if R's most recent partner was a former wife or is a current wife from whom R is separated (p1relation = 2 or 4)

Notes : Use recodes MARDAT01 -05.
The month and century-month variables for this event have been suppressed for public use, but are accessible by application to the NCHS Research Data Center. See Appendix 7 of the User's Guide for further information.
